		<category name="No Game Scaling">
			<comment>Makes the game not scale per level.</comment>
			<category name="Code">
				<code profiles="default">set GD_Balance_HealthAndDamage.HealthAndDamage.Att_UniversalBalanceScaler:ConstantAttributeValueResolver_0 ConstantValue 1.0</code>
			</category>
			<category name="No Level Requirement For Gear">
				<comment>Mod written by GitHub: Our Lord And Savior Gabe Newell / Nexus Mods: OB4MA</comment>
				<comment></comment>
				<comment>This mod makes it so that you can use anything that might normally have a level restriction on it, at any player level.</comment>
				<comment></comment>
				<comment>For example you can use an Overpowered 10 Gub at level 1 if you manage to get one somehow.</comment>
				<comment></comment>
				<comment>This lets you focus on stats of items, rather than when can you use it.</comment>
				<category name="Code">
					<category name="Turn back before it is too late.">
